with remote storage systems in four ways:\n158: \n159: - Prometheus can write samples that it ingests to a remote URL in a [Remote Write format](https://prometheus.io/docs/specs/remote_write_spec_2_0/).\n160: - Prometheus can receive samples from other clients in a [Remote Write format](https://github.com/prometheus/prometheus/blob/main/prompb/remote.proto#L31).\n162: - Prometheus can return sample data requested by clients in a [Remote Read
